<script type="text/javascript">
    function initCrazy(crazyUrl, crazyId, width, height, minWidth, wminWidth) {
        var isResponsive = true;
        if (Q.browser.IE6 || Q.browser.IE7) {
          // IE6/7没有响应式
          isResponsive = false;
        }

        var wrapper = document.createElement('div');
        var element = document.createElement('div');
        var ifr = document.createElement('iframe');
        
        var wrapperMinW = wminWidth || 1000;
        var elementMinW = minWidth || 980;
        var elementMaxW = width;
        var elementW = '100%';
        if (!isResponsive) {
          // 非响应式则设定为固定宽度
          elementW = elementMinW + 'px';
        }
        
        wrapper.id = 'crazy' + crazyId;
        wrapper.style.cssText = 'position:absolute;left:0px;top:-5000px;z-index:3000;width:100%;height:' + height + 'px;min-width:' + wrapperMinW + 'px;';
        
        element.id = 'flash' + crazyId;
        element.style.cssText = 'position:relative;z-index:3;width:' + elementW + ';height:100%;margin:0 auto;max-width:' + elementMaxW +'px;min-width:' + elementMinW + 'px;';
        element.innerHTML = createSwfObject(crazyUrl, crazyId, '100%', '100%');
        
        ifr.style.cssText = 'left:0px;top:0px;width:100%;height:100%;position:absolute;z-index:1;background-color:#000';
        
        element.appendChild(ifr);
        wrapper.appendChild(element);
        document.body.appendChild(wrapper);
    }

    function createSwfObject(url, crazyId, width, height) {
        var wm = 'opaque';
        if (Q.browser.SAFARI) {
            wm = 'window';
        }
        var opts = {};
        opts.id = 'adflash' + crazyId;
        opts.width = width;
        opts.height = height;
        opts.params = {
            'wMode': wm
        };
        opts.vars = {
            'playerId': 'flash',
            'creativeId': crazyId
        };
        opts.styles = {
            'position': 'absolute',
            'z-index': '2'
        };
        
        return Q.flash.create(url, opts);            
    }

    function showCrazy(crazyId) {        
      var top = Q.$('#flash').top() + 1; // 错位1像素可使底下的播放器露出来从而避免在FF等浏览器上因flash被遮盖而代码不执行的bug，UI上不影响
        var wrapper = document.getElementById('crazy' + crazyId);
        if (wrapper) {
            wrapper.style.top = top + 'px';
        }
    }
    
    function resizeCrazy(crazyId, width, height) {
        var wrapper = document.getElementById('crazy' + crazyId);
        var element = document.getElementById('flash' + crazyId);
        if (wrapper) {
          wrapper.style.height = height + 'px';
        }
        if (element) {
          element.style.maxWidth = width + 'px';
        }
    }

    function closeCrazy(crazyId) {
        var wrapper = document.getElementById('crazy' + crazyId);
        if (wrapper) {
            wrapper.innerHTML = '';
            document.body.removeChild(wrapper);
        }
    }
</script>

  (function () {
    if(!(Q.browser.IE6||Q.browser.IE7)){
    var body = Q.$('body');
    var width = Q.page.getViewWidth() > Q.page.getWidth() ? Q.page.getWidth() : Q.page.getViewWidth();
    if (Q && Q.PageInfo && Q.PageInfo.respInfo) {
      var cnf = Q.PageInfo.respInfo.cnf;
      body.removeClass(cnf[Q.PageInfo.respInfo.curLayout].cls);
      for (var i = 0; i < cnf.length; i++) {
        if (width >= cnf[i].range.min && width <= cnf[i].range.max && !body.hasClass(cnf[i].cls)) {
          body.addClass(cnf[i].cls);
          Q.PageInfo.respInfo.curLayout = cnf[i].layout;
          break;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  })();

<script type="text/javascript">
  /* 高度：更新策略、vip、活动消息、标题及其他、选集标题 */
  /* 高度：更新策略、vip、活动消息、标题及其他、选集标题 */

  var _tabtag = Q('.J_drama_tabtag');

  /* 列表 */
  var _tabscroll = Q('.J_drama_scroll');
  /* 当前响应布局 */
  var resp = Q.PageInfo && Q.PageInfo.respInfo || {};
  var curlay = resp.curLayout || 0;
  var layout = resp.cnf[curlay] || {};
  /* 右侧总高度 */
  var allHeight = layout.extraInfo.rightWrapHeight;//_wholeTable.outerHeight(false)|| 417;

  /* 目标高度 */
  var _H = allHeight;
  var tabH = _tabtag.outerHeight(true);
  _H = _H - tabH;
  //_H = _H - 20;
  _H = _H + 'px';
  if(_tabscroll){
    _tabscroll.height(_H);
  }
</script>

  (function(){
    function change(){
      var current = index++%domsarr.length;
      for (var i = 0; i < domsarr.length; i++) {
        var tempEl = domsarr[i];
        if(i===current){
          if(current==1){
            tempEl.css("height","");
            tempEl.css("visibility","visible");
            tempEl.show();
          }else{
            tempEl.show();
          }
        }else{
          if(i==1){
            tempEl.css("height",0);
            tempEl.css("visibility","hidden");
          }else{
            tempEl.hide();
          }
        }
        
      }
    }
    var domsarr = [];
    Q.$('#widget-appdown-random1')&&domsarr.push(Q.$('#widget-appdown-random1'));
    !Q.browser.iPad&&Q.$("#widget-randomad-container")&&domsarr.push(Q.$("#widget-randomad-container"));
    var len = domsarr.length;
    if(len){
      var index = parseInt((Math.random()) * domsarr.length, 10);
      setInterval(function(){
        change();
      },1000*60*10);
      change();
    }
  })();
